"PKG INIT"DYNAMIC_LOV_ITM_AVL_QTY"P_I_CODE"P_W_CODE"V_WHR"V_SQL""
DYNAMIC_LOV_ITM_AVL_QTY
 SELECT I_CODE,Decode(
,1,Nvl(I_Name,I_E_Name),Nvl(I_E_Name,I_Name)) I_Name,itm_unt,W_Code,Expire_Date,Batch_No,ITM_QTY
	    FROM (
	    Select A.I_Code,A.W_Code,Decode(Expire_Date,'01/01/1900','',Expire_Date) Expire_Date,
	               Decode(Batch_No, '0','', Batch_No) Batch_No,A.Avl_Qty ITM_QTY
	              From IAS_ITM_MST M,IAS_ITM_DTL D,MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY A
	              WHERE M.I_CODE=D.I_CODE
	              AND D.I_CODE=A.I_CODE 
	              AND Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
 And I_Code=
 And W_Code=
 Order By I_Code,w_code

SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,AVL_QTY   FROM (SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,AVL_QTY   FROM MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY  WHERE I_CODE = :b1  AND W_CODE = :b2  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') < TO_DATE(:b3,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') >= TO_DATE(:b4,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  AND NVL(AVL_QTY,0) > 0  UNION ALL SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,- SUM(((NVL(I_QTY,0) + NVL(FREE_QTY,0) ) * NVL(P_SIZE,1) ))  AVL_QTY   FROM IAS_POS_HUNG_BILLS  WHERE I_CODE = :b1  AND W_CODE = :b2  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') < TO_DATE(:b3,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') >= TO_DATE(:b4,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  GROUP BY EXPIRE_DATE )  WHERE EXPIRE_DATE < :b3  AND ROWNUM <= 1"SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,AVL_QTY   FROM (SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,AVL_QTY   FROM MV_ITEM_AVL_QTY  WHERE I_CODE = :b1  AND W_CODE = :b2  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') < TO_DATE(:b3,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  AND NVL(AVL_QTY,0) > 0  UNION ALL SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,- SUM(((NVL(I_QTY,0) + NVL(FREE_QTY,0) ) * NVL(P_SIZE,1) ))  AVL_QTY   FROM IAS_POS_BILL_MST M,IAS_POS_BILL_DTL D  WHERE M.BILL_NO = D.BILL_NO  AND NVL(POSTED,0) = 0  AND I_CODE = :b1  AND D.W_CODE = :b2  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') < TO_DATE(:b3,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  GROUP BY EXPIRE_DATE  UNION ALL SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,- SUM(((NVL(I_QTY,0) + NVL(FREE_QTY,0) ) * NVL(P_SIZE,1) ))  AVL_QTY   FROM IAS_POS_HUNG_BILLS  WHERE I_CODE = :b1  AND W_CODE = :b2  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') < TO_DATE(:b3,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  GROUP BY EXPIRE_DATE  UNION ALL SELECT EXPIRE_DATE,SUM(((NVL(I_QTY,0) + NVL(FREE_QTY,0) ) * NVL(P_SIZE,1) )) AVL_QTY   FROM IAS_POS_RT_BILL_MST M,IAS_POS_RT_BILL_DTL D  WHERE M.RT_BILL_NO = D.RT_BILL_NO  AND NVL(POSTED,0) = 0  AND I_CODE = :b1  AND D.W_CODE = :b2  AND TO_DATE(EXPIRE_DATE,''DD/MM/YYYY'') < TO_DATE(:b3,''DD/MM/YYYY'')  GROUP BY EXPIRE_DATE )  WHERE EXPIRE_DATE < :b3  AND ROWNUM <= 1"

(SELECT B.G_CODE GRP_CODE
																														      ,DECODE ( 
, 1, B.G_A_NAME, NVL (B.G_E_NAME, B.G_A_NAME))     GRP_NM
																														      ,GRP_COLOR
																														      ,GRP_FONT_COLOR
																														      ,GRP_ITM_COLOR
																														      ,GRP_ITM_FONT_COLOR
																														  FROM POS_DFLT_GRP_DTL A, GROUP_DETAILS B
																														 WHERE A.GRP_NO(+) = B.G_CODE 
																														   AND EXISTS
																														           (SELECT 1
																														              FROM PRIVILEGE_GC
																														             WHERE 
																														                   OR U_ID = 
																														                      AND G_CODE = B.G_CODE
																														                      AND ADD_FLAG = 1
																														                      AND ROWNUM <= 1)
																														   AND EXISTS
																														                (SELECT 1
																														                   FROM IAS_ITEM_PRICE C, IAS_ITM_MST D
																														                  WHERE C.I_CODE = D.I_CODE
																														                        AND B.G_CODE = D.G_CODE
																														                        AND C.LEV_NO = 
																														                        AND ROWNUM <= 1))

SELECT B.I_CODE,B.ITM_UNT,SUM(NVL(C.I_QTY,1)) I_QTY,AVG(NVL(C.CPN_AMT,0)) CPN_AMT   FROM IAS_CPN_TYP_MST A,IAS_CPN_TYP_DTL B,POS_BILL_CPN C,IAS_POS_BILL_DTL D  WHERE A.CPN_TYP_NO = B.CPN_TYP_NO  AND A.CPN_TYP_NO = C.CPN_TYP_NO  AND B.CPN_TYP_NO = C.CPN_TYP_NO  AND B.I_CODE = D.I_CODE  AND B.ITM_UNT = D.ITM_UNT  AND C.BILL_NO = D.BILL_NO  AND A.CPN_USE_MTHD = 2  AND A.CPN_RPLC_MTHD = 2  AND D.BILL_NO = :b1  GROUP BY B.I_CODE,B.ITM_UNT"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_DTL SET CPN_QTY=0 WHERE BILL_NO = :b1"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_MST SET CPN_DIFF_AMT=0 WHERE BILL_NO = :b1"SELECT I_CODE,ITM_UNT,I_QTY,RCRD_NO   FROM IAS_POS_BILL_DTL  WHERE BILL_NO = :b1  AND I_CODE = :b2  AND ITM_UNT = :b3  AND NVL(CPN_QTY,0) < NVL(I_QTY,0) ORDER BY RCRD_NO"SELECT NVL(I_QTY,0) - NVL(CPN_QTY,0)    FROM IAS_POS_BILL_DTL  WHERE BILL_NO = :b1  AND I_CODE = :b2  AND ITM_UNT = :b3  AND RCRD_NO = :b4"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_DTL SET CPN_QTY=I_QTY WHERE BILL_NO = :b1  AND I_CODE = :b2  AND ITM_UNT = :b3  AND RCRD_NO = :b4"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_DTL SET CPN_QTY=:b1 WHERE BILL_NO = :b2  AND I_CODE = :b3  AND ITM_UNT = :b4  AND RCRD_NO = :b5"SELECT 1   FROM IAS_CPN_TYP_MST M,POS_BILL_CPN D  WHERE M.CPN_TYP_NO = D.CPN_TYP_NO  AND M.CPN_USE_MTHD = 2  AND M.CPN_RPLC_MTHD = 2  AND D.BILL_NO = :b1  AND ROWNUM <= 1"SELECT SUM(NVL(C.I_QTY,1))   FROM IAS_CPN_TYP_MST A,POS_BILL_CPN C  WHERE A.CPN_TYP_NO = C.CPN_TYP_NO  AND A.CPN_USE_MTHD = 2  AND A.CPN_RPLC_MTHD = 2  AND C.BILL_NO = :b1"SELECT SUM(NVL(CPN_QTY,0)),ROUND(SUM((NVL(I_QTY,0) - NVL(CPN_QTY,0) ) * (NVL(I_PRICE,0) + NVL(VAT_AMT,0) ) ),:b1)   FROM IAS_POS_BILL_DTL  WHERE BILL_NO = :b2"SELECT SUM(NVL(C.I_QTY,1) * NVL(C.CPN_AMT,0) )   FROM IAS_CPN_TYP_MST A,IAS_CPN_TYP_DTL B,POS_BILL_CPN C  WHERE A.CPN_TYP_NO = B.CPN_TYP_NO  AND A.CPN_TYP_NO = C.CPN_TYP_NO  AND B.CPN_TYP_NO = C.CPN_TYP_NO  AND (A.CPN_USE_MTHD != 2  OR A.CPN_RPLC_MTHD != 2 ) AND C.BILL_NO = :b1"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_MST SET CPN_DIFF_AMT=ROUND(NVL(:b1,0) - RG_C_CODE
Select customer.c_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_a_name, c_e_name),
                Nvl (c_e_name, c_a_name)) c_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_group_a_name, c_group_e_name),
                Nvl (c_group_e_name, c_group_a_name)) group_name,
       customer.c_a_code a_code,C_MOBILE
  From customer,Customer_Group
 Where 
     customer.c_Group_Code = Customer_Group.c_Group_Code(+) 
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = customer.c_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And c_code = customer.c_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
And  customer.c_code Like  Decode(:ias_pos_bill_mst.c_code,Null,'%',:ias_pos_bill_mst.c_code||'%') 
Order By c_code

Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.A_Cy,B.A_CY,I_Price, Round(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_Itm_Price_Docacy (D.I_Code, 
                                  D.Itm_Unt, 
                                  :Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.A_Cy,
                                  :Parameter.Local_Cur,
                                  :Parameter.Stk_Cur,
                                  :Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Rate,                                
                                  Nvl(:Parameter.Stock_Rate,1),
                                  A.Lev_No,:Parameter.Def_Wcode),2)) I_PRICE ,
Round((Ias_Itm_Pkg.Get_Grand_Wtavg (P_Wtavg_Type => :Parameter.Wtavg_Type,
                                   P_Icode      => m.i_code ,                                                  
                                   P_Wcode      => :Parameter.Def_Wcode)*Nvl(D.P_Size,1)*Nvl(:Parameter.stock_rate,1))/Nvl(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Rate,1),2) STK_CST                                  
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D ,IAS_ITEM_PRICE A,Ias_Pricing_Levels b
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
and a.Lev_No   = b.Lev_No
and Nvl(M.Inactive,0)=0 and Nvl(D.NO_SALE,0)=0 
AND M.I_CODE=A.I_CODE
AND D.ITM_UNT=A.ITM_UNT
AND Exists (select 1 from Measurement where Measure_Code = d.itm_unt 
And Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,Nvl(Unt_Sale_Typ,3)) = Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ) ) 
And  Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,A.W_Code,5,A.Brn_No,1) 
               = Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,:Parameter.Def_Wcode,5,:Parameter.Def_Brn_No,1)
AND A.LEV_NO=:Parameter.Price_Level
AND NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),0,0,NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0))
AND NVL(M.USE_ATTCH,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),0,0,NVL(M.USE_ATTCH,0))
And Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=m.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Get_Items_ACtivity(m.Activity_No,
                       :Parameter.User_No       ,
                       :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1

               = Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,:Parameter.Def_Wcode,5,:Parameter.Def_Brn_No,1)

Select c_code, c_name, group_name,a_code,C_MOBILE,Cstmr_Typ,Cstmr_Typ_Nm
From (
Select customer.c_code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_a_name, c_e_name),
                Nvl (c_e_name, c_a_name)) c_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (c_group_a_name, c_group_e_name),
                Nvl (c_group_e_name, c_group_a_name)) group_name,
       customer.c_a_code a_code,C_MOBILE,
       2 Cstmr_Typ,Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_Prompt(:Parameter.lang_no,346) Cstmr_Typ_Nm
  From customer,Customer_Group
 Where 
     customer.c_Group_Code = Customer_Group.c_Group_Code(+) 
AND  customer.c_code Like  Decode(:ias_pos_bill_mst.Cstmr_crdt_csh_code_dmy,Null,'%',:ias_pos_bill_mst.Cstmr_crdt_csh_code_dmy||'%') 
 And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (((:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
          And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Priv_Acc
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And A_Code = customer.c_a_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
 Or ((:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
            And Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From Ias_Priv_customer
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And c_code = customer.c_code
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                      And RowNum <=1 ))))
AND NVL(customer.FDA_CST_FLG,0)=0
Union All 
Select Cust_Code c_code ,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Cust_L_Nm , Cust_F_Nm ),
                Nvl (Cust_F_Nm , Cust_L_Nm )) c_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Cust_GRP_L_NM , Cust_GRP_F_NM ),
                Nvl (Cust_GRP_F_NM,Cust_GRP_L_NM )) group_name,
                 Null a_code,MOBILE_NO C_MOBILE,
     1 Cstmr_Typ,Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_Prompt(:Parameter.lang_no,153) Cstmr_Typ_Nm
  From IAS_CASH_CUSTMR,IAS_CASH_CUSTMR_GRP
 Where IAS_CASH_CUSTMR.Cust_GRP_CODE  = IAS_CASH_CUSTMR_GRP.Cust_GRP_CODE(+) 
AND  IAS_CASH_CUSTMR.cust_code Like  Decode(:ias_pos_bill_mst.Cstmr_crdt_csh_code_dmy,Null,'%',:ias_pos_bill_mst.Cstmr_crdt_csh_code_dmy||'%') 
And (:Parameter.User_No = 1 OR  nvl(:PARAMETER.SHW_CSHCST_BY_BRN,0) =0 OR
  EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                                        WHERE U_ID =:PARAMETER.USER_NO
                                          AND S_BRN_USR_PRIV.BRN_NO     = IAS_CASH_CUSTMR.BRN_NO
                                          AND NVL(VIEW_FLAG, 1) = 1 
                                          AND ROWNUM <= 1)  ) 
Order By c_code,Cstmr_Typ
Select Cust_Code,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Cust_L_Nm , Cust_F_Nm ),
                Nvl (Cust_F_Nm , Cust_L_Nm )) cust_name,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Cust_GRP_L_NM , Cust_GRP_F_NM ),
                Nvl (Cust_GRP_F_NM,Cust_GRP_L_NM )) group_name
  From IAS_CASH_CUSTMR,IAS_CASH_CUSTMR_GRP
 Where IAS_CASH_CUSTMR.Cust_GRP_CODE  = IAS_CASH_CUSTMR_GRP.Cust_GRP_CODE(+) 
And  cust_code Like  Decode(:ias_pos_bill_mst.cust_code,Null,'%',:ias_pos_bill_mst.cust_code||'%') 
And (:Parameter.User_No = 1 OR  nvl(:PARAMETER.SHW_CSHCST_BY_BRN,0) =0 OR
  EXISTS(SELECT 1 FROM S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                                        WHERE U_ID =:PARAMETER.USER_NO
                                          AND S_BRN_USR_PRIV.BRN_NO     = IAS_CASH_CUSTMR.BRN_NO
                                          AND NVL(VIEW_FLAG, 1) = 1 
                                          AND ROWNUM <= 1)  ) 
Order By cust_code

NVL(DISC_AMT_DTL,0)    FROM IAS_POS_BILL_MST  WHERE BILL_NO = :b1  AND ROWNUM <= 1"SELECT 1   FROM IAS_POS_BILL_DTL  WHERE BILL_NO = :b1  AND I_QTY > 0  AND ROWNUM <= 1"SELECT SUM(NVL(FREE_QTY,0) * NVL(I_PRICE,0) )   FROM IAS_POS_BILL_DTL  WHERE BILL_NO = :b1"SELECT COUNT(1)   FROM POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE BILL_NO = :b1  AND DOC_TYPE = 4  AND ROWNUM <= 1"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_DTL A SET OTHR_AMT=(SELECT ROUND(NVL(A.OTHR_AMT,0) + (SUM(NVL(POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.AMT,0)) / NVL(:b1,0) ) * NVL(A.I_PRICE,0)  ,9)   FROM POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.BILL_NO = A.BILL_NO  AND DOC_TYPE = 4  AND POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.BILL_NO = :b2 ) WHERE BILL_NO = :b2  AND NVL(I_QTY,0) > 0"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_DTL A SET OTHR_AMT=(SELECT ROUND(NVL(A.OTHR_AMT,0) + (SUM(NVL(POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.AMT,0)) / NVL(:b1,0) ) * NVL(A.I_PRICE,0)  ,9)   FROM POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.BILL_NO = A.BILL_NO  AND DOC_TYPE = 4  AND POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT.BILL_NO = :b2 ) WHERE BILL_NO = :b2"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_MST SET OTHR_AMT=(SELECT ROUND(NVL(SUM(AMT),0),:b1)   FROM POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE DOC_TYPE = 4  AND BILL_NO = :b2 ) WHERE BILL_NO = :b2"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_MST A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=(SELECT SUM(NVL(VAT_AMT,0))   FROM POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT  WHERE BILL_NO = A.BILL_NO  AND DOC_TYPE = 4  AND BILL_NO = :b1 ) WHERE BILL_NO = :b1"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_DTL A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=(SELECT ROUND((NVL(IAS_POS_BILL_MST.VAT_AMT_OTHR,0) / NVL(IAS_POS_BILL_MST.BILL_AMT,0) ) * NVL(A.I_PRICE,0) ,9)   FROM IAS_POS_BILL_MST  WHERE BILL_NO = A.BILL_NO  AND BILL_NO = :b1 ) WHERE BILL_NO = :b1"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_MST A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=0 WHERE BILL_NO = :b1"UPDATE IAS_POS_BILL_DTL A SET VAT_AMT_OTHR=0 WHERE BILL_NO = :b1"UPDATE POS_OTHR_CHRG_MVMNT A SET VAT_PRCNT=0,VAT_AMT=0 WHERE DOC_TYPE = 4  AND BILL_NO = :b1"

Round(Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.A_Cy,:Parameter.Local_Cur,A.I_PRICE,A.I_PRICE/Nvl(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Rate,1)),:Parameter.No_Of_Decimal)  I_PRICE
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D ,IAS_ITEM_PRICE A
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
and Nvl(M.Inactive,0)=0 and Nvl(D.NO_SALE,0)=0 
AND M.I_CODE=A.I_CODE
AND D.ITM_UNT=A.ITM_UNT
AND Exists (select 1 from Measurement where Measure_Code = d.Itm_unt 
And Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,Nvl(Unt_Sale_Typ,3)) In(Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ),3) )
And  Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,A.W_Code,5,A.Brn_No,1) 
               = Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,:Parameter.Def_Wcode,5,:Parameter.Def_Brn_No,1)
AND A.LEV_NO=:Parameter.Price_Level
AND NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),0,0,NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0))
AND NVL(M.USE_ATTCH,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),0,0,NVL(M.USE_ATTCH,0))
And Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=m.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Get_Items_ACtivity(m.Activity_No,
                       :Parameter.User_No       ,
                       :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1
And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2, upper(M.I_Name||M.I_Desc||M.I_E_Name),
                3,upper(M.I_Code||M.I_Name||M.I_E_Name),
                M.I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
order by m.i_code,i_name

From Ars_Fda_Itm_Lst_Dtl_Tmp
 Where Ars_Fda_Itm_Lst_Dtl_Tmp.I_Code=IAS_V_ITM_AVL_QTY.I_Code
  And REFERENCE_NUMBER=:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Fda_Code 
  And Nvl(NET_QTY,0)>0
 And RowNum<=1)
AND W_CODE =DECODE(NVL(:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE,0),0,W_CODE,:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE)
And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                3,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
order by i_code,To_Date(Expire_Date,'DD/MM/RRRR'),W_CODE
select i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,
decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_e_name,i_name),nvl(i_name,i_e_name)) i_name_f,
itm_unt,W_Code,to_date(Expire_Date,'dd/mm/RRRR') Expire_Date,Batch_No,AVL_QTY
From IAS_V_ITM_AVL_QTY
 Where
 (:Parameter.chck_avl_qty<>1 or nvl(avl_qty,0)>0  )
And Exists(Select 1  
 From Inv_Fda_Itm iFda , Wsfty_Drug_List Drg_Lst
 Where iFda.Fda_Code = Drg_Lst.Barcode 
 And iFda.I_Code    = IAS_V_ITM_AVL_QTY.I_Code
 And RowNum<=1)
AND W_CODE =DECODE(NVL(:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE,0),0,W_CODE,:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE)
And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                3,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
order by i_code,To_Date(Expire_Date,'DD/MM/RRRR'),W_CODE
select i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,
decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_e_name,i_name),nvl(i_name,i_e_name)) i_name_f,
itm_unt,W_Code,to_date(Expire_Date,'dd/mm/RRRR') Expire_Date,Batch_No,AVL_QTY
From IAS_V_ITM_AVL_QTY
 Where
 nvl(avl_qty,0)>0 
And Exists(Select 1  
 From Inv_Fda_Itm_Lst_Mst fM , Inv_Fda_Itm_Lst_Dtl fD
 Where fM.Doc_Ser = fD.Doc_Ser
 And fD.I_Code    = IAS_V_ITM_AVL_QTY.I_Code
 And fM.Mnth    = To_Char(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date,'MM')
 And Nvl(fM.Inactive,0) = 0
 And RowNum<=1)
AND W_CODE =DECODE(NVL(:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE,0),0,W_CODE,:PARAMETER.DEF_WCODE)
And Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                2,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                3,upper(I_Code||I_Name||I_E_Name),
                I_Code) Like
            Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,
                   Null, '%',
                   '%'|| Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,2,Replace(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,' ','%'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code) || '%')
order by i_code,To_Date(Expire_Date,'DD/MM/RRRR'),W_CODE
select m.i_code,decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name,d.itm_unt unit,P_Size,M.i_desc
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
And Nvl(m.service_itm,0)=0
and nvl(d.no_sale,0)=0
and nvl(m.BLOCKED,0)=0
and Nvl(d.INACTIVE,0)=0
AND Exists (select 1 from Measurement where Measure_Code = d.itm_unt 
And Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,Nvl(Unt_Sale_Typ,3)) In(Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ),3) )
and Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=M.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Get_Items_ACtivity(M.Activity_No,
                       :Parameter.User_No       ,
                       :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1
and M.I_CODE=:Ias_pos_bill_dtl.i_code
order by Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,i_name,i_e_name),m.i_code
Select bank_no ,
       bank_name 
  From cash_at_bank 
   Where Exists ( Select 1     From priv_cash 
      Where cash_at_bank.bank_no = priv_cash.cash_no
       And cash_type=2
       And u_id=:Parameter.User_no 
       And Nvl(add_flag,0)=1 
       And RowNum <= 1 )
 Order By bank_no
select decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name, m.i_code,d.itm_unt unit,m.i_desc ,A.I_PRICE,M.VNDR_I_CODE
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D ,IAS_ITEM_PRICE A
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
and Nvl(M.Inactive,0)=0 and Nvl(D.NO_SALE,0)=0 
AND M.I_CODE=A.I_CODE
AND D.ITM_UNT=A.ITM_UNT
AND Exists (select 1 from Measurement where Measure_Code = d.Itm_unt 
And Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,Nvl(Unt_Sale_Typ,3)) In(Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ),3) )
And  Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,A.W_Code,5,A.Brn_No,1) 
               = Decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,:Parameter.Def_Wcode,5,:Parameter.Def_Brn_No,1)
AND A.LEV_NO=:Parameter.Price_Level
AND NVL(M.USE_BATCH_NO,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),0,0,NVL(M.USE_BATCH_NO,0))
AND NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),0,0,NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0))
AND NVL(M.USE_ATTCH,0)=0
And Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=m.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)
And Get_Items_ACtivity(m.Activity_No,
                       :Parameter.User_No       ,
                       :Parameter.Conn_Itm_Act_By_Usr_Priv) = 1
and decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,I_name,i_e_name) Like decode(:ias_pos_bill_dtl.i_code,Null,'%','%'||:ias_pos_bill_dtl.i_code||'%')
order by Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,i_name,i_e_name),m.i_code
select decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,1,nvl(i_name,i_e_name),nvl(i_e_name,i_name)) i_name, m.i_code,d.itm_unt unit,m.i_desc ,A.I_PRICE,M.VNDR_I_CODE
From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D ,IAS_ITEM_PRICE A
 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
and Nvl(M.Inactive,0)=0 and Nvl(D.NO_SALE,0)=0 
AND NVL(M.USE_BATCH_NO,0)=0 
AND M.I_CODE=A.I_CODE
AND D.ITM_UNT=A.ITM_UNT

AND A.LEV_NO=:Parameter.Price_Level
AND NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0)=Decode(Nvl(:Parameter.post_itm_frst_expdate,0),1,NVL(M.USE_EXP_DATE,0),0)
AND NVL(M.USE_ATTCH,0)=0
And Exists (select 1 from privilege_gc where u_id=:Parameter.User_no and g_code=m.g_code and add_flag=1 and RowNum<=1)

                       :Parameter.User_No       ,

 Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code

And  m.I_Code = a.I_Code
And  d.I_Code = a.I_Code

And RowNum <= 1 )
and m.i_code like  Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,Null,'%',:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code||'%')

            DECODE (a.batch_no, '0', '', a.batch_no) batch_no 
 from ias_itm_mst m,Ias_Itm_Dtl D,Ias_Itm_Unt_Barcode a

And RowNum <= 1 )
and m.i_code like  Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,Null,'%',:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code||'%')

RG_ITM_UNT
Select   D.Itm_Unt,
         Lvl_Unit,
 Round(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_Itm_Price_Docacy(M.I_Code,
                                         D.Itm_Unt,
                                                :Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.a_cy,
                                                :Parameter.Local_Cur,
                                                :Parameter.Stk_Cur,                                                     :Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Rate,
                                                :Parameter.STOCK_RATE,
                                                :Parameter.Price_Level,
                                                 :Parameter.Def_Wcode,
                                                 null,
                                                 1,
                                                 :Parameter.Price_Type),2) I_Price,
         P_Size
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D 
   Where M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And D.I_Code = :IAS_POS_BILL_DTL.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.NO_SALE,0)=0
     And Nvl(D.INACTIVE,0)=0
AND Exists (select 1 from Measurement where Measure_Code = d.Itm_unt 
And Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,Nvl(Unt_Sale_Typ,3)) In(Decode(:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ,3,0,:Parameter.Wcode_Sale_Typ),3) )
and Exists (select 1 from IAS_ITEM_PRICE
 where i_code=m.i_code and Itm_Unt=D.Itm_Unt and nvl(I_PRICE,0)>0 and RowNum<=1)
Order By Lvl_Unit

RG_I_PRICE
Select Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No,
       Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,1, Nvl (Lev_A_Name, Lev_E_Name), Nvl (Lev_E_Name, Lev_A_Name)) L_Name,
       A_Cy,  
       I_Price, 
        Decode(A_Cy,:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.A_Cy,I_Price, Round(Ias_Gen_Pkg.Get_Itm_Price_Docacy (:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code, 
                                  :Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.Itm_Unt, 
                                  :Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.A_Cy,
                                  :Parameter.Local_Cur,
                                  :Parameter.Stk_Cur,
                                  :Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Rate,                                
                                  Nvl(:Parameter.Stock_Rate,1),
                                  Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No,:Parameter.Def_Wcode),2)) Sale_Price
  From Ias_Item_Price, Ias_Pricing_Levels
 Where Ias_Item_Price.I_Code = :Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code
   And Ias_Item_Price.Itm_unt = :Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.Itm_unt
   And Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No = Ias_Pricing_Levels.Lev_No
   And ((:Parameter.User_No = 1 ) 
         Or (Exists (
          Select Lev_No
            From Ias_Priv_Price
           Where U_Id   = :Parameter.User_No
             And Lev_No = Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No
             And Nvl (Add_Flag, 0) = 1 And Rownum<=1 )))
     and nvl(Ias_Item_Price.w_code,0)=decode(:Parameter.Price_Type,2,:Parameter.Def_Wcode,nvl(Ias_Item_Price.w_code,0))   
 Order By Ias_Item_Price.Lev_No

L_NAME
I_PRICE
SALE_PRICE

         Sales_Order.Order_No, 
         Sales_Order.Order_Date, 
         Sales_Order.C_Name,
         Sales_Order.A_Desc,        
         Sales_Order.Ref_Doc_No, 
         Sales_Order.Order_Ser, 
         Sales_Order.Brn_No,
         Nvl(CSH_PYMNT_AMT,0)+Nvl(Cr_Card_Amt,0)+Nvl(Cr_Card_Amt_Scnd,0)+Nvl(Cr_Card_Amt_Thrd,0)          ADVNC_PYMNT_AMT
    From Sales_Order
   Where (NVL(Sales_Order.Procesed,0) = 0  Or nvl(Sales_Order.EXPORT,0)=1)
     And Sales_Order.Approved = 1
     And (   (:Parameter.User_No = 1)
          Or Exists(
                Select 1
                  From S_Brn_Usr_Priv
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And S_Brn_Usr_Priv.Brn_No = Sales_Order.Brn_No
                   And Nvl(Fill_Flag, 1) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1))
Order By Sales_Order.So_Type, Sales_Order.Order_No

RG_AC_CODE
Select   A_Code, Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,
                        1, A_Name,
                        Nvl(A_Name_Eng, A_Name)) A_Name,  
         Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,
                1, Group_Name,
                Group_E_Name) Group_Name
    From Account, Account_Grouping
   Where Account.A_Grouping = Account_Grouping.Group_No(+)
     And Nvl(Account.Ac_Dtl_Typ,0)=Decode(:ias_pos_bill_mst.AC_DTL_TYP,7,7,0)
     And Exists(Select Account_Type
                  From Account_Types
                 Where Nvl(Affected_By_Trans, 0) = 1 And Account_Type = Account.A_S_M)
     And Exists(
            Select 1
              From Priv_Acc
             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
               And A_Code = Account.A_Code
               And Add_Flag = 1
               And Rownum <= 1)
     And A_Code Like Decode(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Ac_Code,
                            Null, '%',
                            :Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Ac_Code || '%')
Order By Decode(:Parameter.P_Ord_Lov,
                 1, A_Code,
                Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,
                       1, A_Name,
                       A_Name_Eng))

RG_EMP_NO_AC
Select EMP_NO,
       Decode (:Parameter.lang_dflt,1, Nvl (EMP_L_NM, EMP_F_NM),
                Nvl (EMP_F_NM, EMP_L_NM)) emp_name
  From S_EMP
 Where  ((:Parameter.User_No = 1)
        Or (( Exists (
                   Select 1
                     From S_BRN_USR_PRIV
                    Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                      And brn_no= S_EMP.brn_no
                      And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1 
                      And RowNum <=1 ))
And  s_emp.EMP_NO Like  Decode(:Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.ac_code_dtl,Null,'%',:Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.ac_code_dtl||'%') 
AND Nvl(Inactive,0)=0
AND ((:Parameter.User_No = 1 )
        Or 1 =   (Case When :Parameter.EMP_PRV_TYP = 0
                                         Then 1
                                      Else (Select 1
                                              From S_Emp_Prv
                                             Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                                               And Empno_Hrchyno =
                                                      Decode (:Parameter.EMP_PRV_TYP,
                                                              1, S_EMP.Emp_No,
                                                              2, S_EMP.Hrchy_No
                                                             )
                                               And         Add_Flag=1              
                                               And Rownum <= 1)
                                   End) )
Order By EMP_NO

RG_V_CODE_AC
SELECT V_DETAILS.V_CODE,
       DECODE (:PARAMETER.lang_dflt,1, NVL (V_A_NAME, V_E_NAME),
                NVL (V_E_NAME, V_A_NAME)) V_NAME,
       V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE A_CODE
  FROM V_DETAILS
 WHERE V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE=NVL(:IAS_POS_BILL_MST.AC_CODE,V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE)
AND ((:PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1)
        OR (((:PARAMETER.APALT = 1)
          AND EXISTS (
                   SELECT 1
                     FROM PRIV_ACC
                    WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                      AND A_CODE = V_DETAILS.V_A_CODE
                      AND NVL(ADD_FLAG,0) = 1 
                      AND ROWNUM <=1 ))
 OR ((:PARAMETER.APALT = 2)
            AND EXISTS (
                   SELECT 1
                     FROM IAS_PRIV_VENDOR
                    WHERE U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                      AND V_CODE = V_DETAILS.V_CODE
                      AND NVL(ADD_FLAG,0) = 1
                      AND ROWNUM <=1 ))))
AND  V_CODE LIKE  DECODE(:IAS_POS_BILL_MST.AC_CODE_DTL,NULL,'%',:IAS_POS_BILL_MST.AC_CODE_DTL||'%') 
ORDER BY LPAD(V_CODE,15,'0')

RG_LOV_LST
Select   Customer.C_Code,
         Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,
                1, Nvl(C_A_Name, C_E_Name),
                Nvl(C_E_Name, C_A_Name)) C_Name,
         Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,
                1, Nvl(C_Group_A_Name, C_Group_E_Name),
                Nvl(C_Group_E_Name, C_Group_A_Name)) C_Group_Name,
         C_Phone,
         C_Address
    From Customer,        
         Customer_Group
   Where Customer.C_Group_Code = Customer_Group.C_Group_Code(+)    
     And (   (:Parameter.User_No = 1)
          Or (   (    (:Parameter.Aralt = 1)
                  And Exists(
                         Select 1
                           From Priv_Acc
                          Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                            And A_Code = Customer.C_A_Code
                            And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
                            And Rownum <= 1))
              Or (    (:Parameter.Aralt = 2)
                  And Exists(
                         Select 1
                           From Ias_Priv_Customer
                          Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                            And C_Code = Customer.C_Code
                            And Nvl(Add_Flag, 0) = 1
                            And Rownum <= 1))))
     And C_Code Like Decode(:Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.Ac_code_dtl,
                            Null, '%',
                            :Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.Ac_code_dtl|| '%')
Order By Lpad( C_Code,'30',0),
         Decode(:Parameter.Lang_No,
                1, Nvl(C_A_Name, C_E_Name),
                Nvl(C_E_Name, C_A_Name))
Select   D.Ac_Code_Dtl, D.Ac_Dtl_Typ,
         Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,
                 1, Nvl (Ac_Code_Dtl_L_Nm, Ac_Code_Dtl_F_Nm),
                 Nvl (Ac_Code_Dtl_F_Nm, Ac_Code_Dtl_L_Nm)
                ) Ac_Code_Dtl_Nm,
         Decode (:Parameter.Lang_No,
                 1, Nvl (Grp_L_Nm, Grp_F_Nm),
                 Nvl (Grp_F_Nm, Grp_L_Nm)
                ) Grp_Nm,
         D.Ac_Code Ac_Code
    From Gls_Accnt_Dtl D, Gls_Ac_Code_Dtl_Grps M
   Where D.Grp_Code = M.Grp_Code
     And D.Ac_Dtl_Typ = M.Ac_Dtl_Typ
     And D.Ac_Dtl_Typ=:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Ac_Dtl_Typ
     And (   (:Parameter.User_No = 1)
          Or Exists (
                Select 1
                  From Gls_Accnt_Dtl_Priv
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And Ac_Code_Dtl = D.Ac_Code_Dtl
                   And Nvl (Add_Flag, 0) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1)
         )
Order By Lpad (Ac_Code_Dtl, 30, '0')

RG_MAINSUBG_CODE
SELECT   MNG_CODE,
         DECODE (:PARAMETER.Lang_no,1, NVL (MNG_A_NAME, MNG_E_NAME),NVL (MNG_E_NAME, MNG_A_NAME)) G_NAME
    FROM IAS_MAINSUB_GRP_DTL
   WHERE NVL (G_CODE, '0') = NVL (:PARAMTRS_SRCH.G_CODE, NVL (G_CODE, '0'))
     AND (   :PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1
          OR EXISTS (SELECT G_CODE
                       FROM PRIVILEGE_GC
                      WHERE NVL (ADD_FLAG, 0) = 1
                        AND U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                        AND G_CODE = IAS_MAINSUB_GRP_DTL.G_CODE
                        AND ROWNUM <= 1)
         )
ORDER BY MNG_CODE
MNG_CODE

RG_SUBG_CODE
SELECT   SUBG_CODE,
         DECODE (:PARAMETER.Lang_no,1, NVL (SUBG_A_NAME, SUBG_E_NAME),NVL (SUBG_E_NAME, SUBG_A_NAME)) G_NAME
    FROM IAS_SUB_GRP_DTL
   WHERE NVL (G_CODE, '0') = NVL (:PARAMTRS_SRCH.G_CODE, NVL (G_CODE, '0'))
     AND NVL (MNG_CODE, '0') = NVL (:PARAMTRS_SRCH.MNG_CODE,NVL (MNG_CODE, '0'))
     AND (   :PARAMETER.USER_NO = 1
          OR EXISTS (SELECT G_CODE
                       FROM PRIVILEGE_GC
                      WHERE NVL (ADD_FLAG, 0) = 1
                        AND U_ID = :PARAMETER.USER_NO
                        AND G_CODE = IAS_SUB_GRP_DTL.G_CODE
                        AND ROWNUM <= 1)
         )
ORDER BY SUBG_CODE

RG_CPN
Select D.Cpn_No,
       D.I_PRICE*NVL(D.I_QTY,1) CPN_AMT,
       D.PAID_AMT,
       D.USE_MLTI_FLG
    From Ias_Cpn_Dtl D,Ias_Cpn_Typ_Mst A
    Where D.Cpn_Typ_No=A.Cpn_Typ_No
     AND (Nvl(CPN_CLSS,0)=2 Or NVL(SAL_FLG,0)=1)
     AND (NVL(D.PRCSSD_FLG,0)=0 Or ( USE_MLTI_FLG=1 And ( Nvl(D.I_Price,0)-((nvl(D.I_Price,0)*nvl(D.dis_per,0))/100))-NVL(D.PAID_AMT,0)>0) )
     AND NVL(D.INACTIVE,0) = 0     
And Nvl(D.EXP_DATE,'01/01/1900')>=DECODE(D.EXP_DATE,NULL,Nvl(D.EXP_DATE,'01/01/1900'),:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date)
 ANd (Nvl(a.USE_BOOK_NO,0)=0 Or nvl(BOOK_CONN_CSTMR,0)=0 
OR Exists(Select 1 From IAS_SAL_CPN_MST mc,IAS_SAL_CPN_DTL dc
 Where Mc.Doc_Ser=Dc.Doc_Ser
 And Dc.Cpn_Book_No=D.Cpn_Book_No		
 And Nvl(Mc.C_Code,'0')=Nvl(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.C_Code,Nvl(Mc.C_Code,'0'))
 And RowNum<=1))
 Order By D.Cpn_No 
CPN_NO
CPN_AMT
PAID_AMT
USE_MLTI_FLG

 ANd (Nvl(a.USE_BOOK_NO,0)=0 Or nvl(BOOK_CONN_CSTMR,0)=0
 OR Exists(Select 1 From IAS_SAL_CPN_MST mc,IAS_SAL_CPN_DTL dc
  Where Mc.Doc_Ser=Dc.Doc_Ser

   And RowNum<=1))
Order By M.Book_No

RG_QUT_PRM_DTL
Select Quot_No,
       F_Date,
       T_Date,
       IAS_Gen_Pkg.Get_Flg_Nm (P_flg_code => 'QT_PRM_TYP',P_flg_value => QT_PRM_TYPE,P_Lng_no => :Parameter.Lang_No) QT_PRM_TYPE,
       IAS_Gen_Pkg.Get_Flg_Nm (P_flg_code => 'QT_PRM_METHOD',P_flg_value => QT_PRM_METHOD,P_Lng_no => :Parameter.Lang_No) QT_PRM_METHOD,
       A_Desc,
       Quot_ser
  From Ias_Qut_Prm_Mst 
 Where Quot_No like '%'||:Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.Dmy_Qt_Prm_No||'%'
   and :ias_pos_bill_mst.Bill_Date between f_date and t_date
   and Nvl(inactive,0)=0
   and Nvl(APPROVED,0)= 1
   and Nvl(Use_qtn_prm_in_pos_sys_flg,0)=1
   and Quot_ser In (Select Quot_ser From Table(Ias_qt_prm_pkg.Dyn_qt_prm_dup_ic_vw (  P_date             => :Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.Bill_Date,
                                                                                    P_icode              => :Ias_pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code,
                                                                                   P_itm_unt             => :Ias_pos_Bill_Dtl.itm_unt,
                                                                                   P_wcode               => :Parameter.def_wcode,
                                                                                    P_batch_no           => :Ias_pos_Bill_Dtl.batchno,
                                                                                    P_exp_date           => :Ias_pos_Bill_Dtl.expiredate,
                                                                                    P_bill_doc_type      => :Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.bill_type,
                                                                                    P_c_code             => :Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.c_code,
                                                                                    P_c_code_csh         => :Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.cust_code,
                            P_Chk_Qt_No      => Nvl(Nvl(:Ias_pos_Bill_Dtl.Dmy_Qt_Prm_No,:Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.Dmy_Qt_Prm_No),0),
                            P_Chk_Qt_Ser     => Nvl(Nvl(:Ias_pos_Bill_Dtl.Dmy_Qt_Prm_Ser,:Ias_pos_Bill_Mst.Dmy_Qt_Prm_Ser),0),
                            P_Sys_Typ             => 80,
                            P_lang_no             => :Parameter.Lang_No) ))
Order By Ad_Date Desc

RG_ALT_ITM
Select   A.I_Code_Altntv I_CODE,  
         Decode(:Parameter.lang_dflt,1,Nvl(M.I_Name,M.I_E_Name),Nvl(M.I_E_Name,M.I_Name)) I_Name,  
         A.Itm_Unt_Altntv ITM_UNT,
         Decode(:Parameter.User_No,1,
                 Get_Icode_Avlqty (A.I_Code_Altntv,D.P_Size,Nvl(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.W_Code,:Ias_Pos_Bill_DTL.W_Code)),
                 Get_Icode_Avlqty_Priv (A.I_Code_Altntv, D.P_Size,Nvl(:Ias_Pos_Bill_Mst.W_Code,:Ias_Pos_Bill_DTL.W_Code),
                 :Parameter.User_No)) Avl_Qty, 
         P.I_Price I_Price,
         M.I_Desc,
         M.Group_No,
         M.Vndr_I_Code
    From Ias_Itm_Mst M,Ias_Itm_Dtl D,Ias_Itm_Altrntv A,Ias_Item_Price P
    Where A.I_Code=:Ias_Pos_Bill_Dtl.I_Code
     And M.I_Code=D.I_Code
     And A.I_Code_Altntv=M.I_Code
     And A.I_Code_Altntv=D.I_Code
     And Nvl(D.Main_Unit,0)=1
     And Nvl(D.No_Sale,0) = 0    
     And A.I_Code_Altntv=P.I_Code(+)
     And A.Itm_Unt_Altntv=P.Itm_Unt(+)
     And P.Lev_No(+) =:Parameter.Price_Level
     And (:Parameter.User_No=1 Or Exists (Select 1
                 From Privilege_Gc
                 Where U_Id = :Parameter.User_No
                   And G_Code = M.G_Code
                   And Nvl(Add_Flag,0) = 1
                   And Rownum <= 1))   
Order By A.Ordr_No
